<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нежность.html>не́жность</a> (4812)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">néžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежность.html>не́жность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">néžnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежность.html>не́жности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежность.html>не́жности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежность.html>не́жностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tenderness, caress, fondness, delicacy</li>
<li><i>(plural)</i> kind words, endearments</li></ol>

***нежный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жный</a> (2192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нега.html>не́га</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">néga</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">luxury, comfort, prosperity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">néžnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)нежне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)нежне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gentle, tender
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1847</b>,  Ivan Turgenev,  <cite>It Tears Where It is Thin</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слыть.html>слыву́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:насмешливый.html>насме́шливого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>холо́дного</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́д</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:репутация.html>репута́цией</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:легко.html>легко́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a>… <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вчера.html>вчера́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>пришло́сь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прикинуться.html>прики́нуться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:озабоченный.html>озабо́ченным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жным</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Já slyvú za čelovéka nasméšlivovo i xolódnovo, i óčenʹ étomu rad: s takój reputácijej lexkó žitʹ… no včerá mne prišlósʹ prikínutʹsja ozabóčennym i <b>néžnym</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have a reputation as a mocking and cold person, and I’m very happy about it. It is easy to live with such a reputation… but yesterday I had to pretend to be concerned and <b>gentle</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>fond <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + instrumental, of</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>delicate, soft, fine
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1966</b>,  Vladimir Tendryakov,  <cite>Onega</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлебать.html>хлеба́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горячий.html>горя́чую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>уху́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прямо.html>пря́мо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:есть.html>е́ли</a> разва́ренное <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жное</a></b> нали́мье <a href = vnd.unilang:мясо.html>мя́со</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My xlebáli gorjáčuju uxú, prjámo rukámi jéli razvárennoje <b>néžnoje</b> nalímʹje mjáso.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We gulped down hot ukha and ate <b>delicate</b>, boiled burbot meat with our bare hands.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1877</b>,  Vsevolod Garshin,  <cite>Four Days</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">тёмно-си́нее <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посереть.html>посере́ло</a>, подёрнулось <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жными</a></b> пе́ристыми <a href = vnd.unilang:облачко.html>облачка́ми</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tjómno-síneje nébo poserélo, podjórnulosʹ <b>néžnymi</b> péristymi oblačkámi.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The dark blue sky grayed and became covered with <b>soft</b> cirrus clouds.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1898</b>,  Aleksandr Kuprin,  <cite>Olesya</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поглядеть.html>погляде́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбоку.html>сбо́ку</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:виденный.html>ви́ден</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чистый.html>чи́стый</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:профиль.html>про́филь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слегка.html>слегка́</a> наклонённой <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́ловы</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja pogljadél na nejó sbóku, tak što mne stal víden čístyj, <b>néžnyj</b> prófilʹ jejó slexká naklonjónnoj gólovy.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I eyed her from the side so that the clean, <b>fine</b> profile of her bent-over head easily became visible to me.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>gentle, delicate, tender <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">sensitive or painful</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1830</b>,  Alexander Pushkin,  <cite>The Belkin Tales</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:затруднять.html>затрудня́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:попробовать.html>попро́бовала</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пройти.html>пройти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двору́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:босой.html>бо́сая</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерн.html>дёрн</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колоть.html>коло́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:песок.html>песо́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:камушек.html>ка́мушки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:показаться.html>показа́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нестерпимый.html>нестерпи́мы</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Odnó zatrudnjálo jejó: oná popróbovala býlo projtí po dvorú bósaja, no djórn kolól jejó <b>néžnyje</b> nógi, a pesók i kámuški pokazálisʹ jej nesterpímy.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">One thing caused her difficulty: she tried to walk across the yard barefoot, but the sod pricked her <b>gentle</b> feet and the sand and pebbles appeared unbearable to her.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="переносное значение">перен.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:тонкий.html>то́нкий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> лёгкий, <a href = vnd.unilang:изящный.html>изя́щный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приятный.html>прия́тный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:резкий.html>ре́зкий</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грубый.html>гру́бый</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

***незабудка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:незабудка.html>незабу́дка</a> (26599)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1778. From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">don't</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>забу́дь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zabúdʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">forget</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, an All-European calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">ne m'oubliez mie</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Vergissmeinnicht</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:незабудка.html>незабу́дка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nezabúdka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:незабудка.html>незабу́дки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:незабудка.html>незабу́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:незабудка.html>незабу́док</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> forget-me-not</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:незаметный.html>незаме́тный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nezamétnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>imperceptibly</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:незаметный.html>незаме́тный</a> (6649)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заметный.html>заме́тный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamétnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:незаметный.html>незаме́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nezamétnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)незаме́тнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)незаме́тней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>inconspicuous, invisible, undetectable, unnoticeable</li>
<li>plain, ordinary, insignificant</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pámjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:незапамятный.html>незапа́мятный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nezapámjatnyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:незаслуженный.html>незаслу́женный</a> (23925)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заслуженный.html>заслу́женный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaslúžennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зрячий.html>зря́чий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zrjáčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:незрячий.html>незря́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nezrjáčij</span>)
</p>
